               <h2 class="pane-title">
                Bingo Games
               </h2>
               <script>
                var ForwardTimerID = {};
 
 function countDown(id, time)
 {
   psecond = time % 60;
   pminute = parseInt((time / 60) % 60);
   phour = parseInt((time / 3600) % 24);
   pday = parseInt(time / (3600 * 24));
   if (pminute == 0 && psecond == 0)
   {
     document.getElementById(id).innerHTML = "Started";
     clearTimeout(ForwardTimerID[id]);
     return;
   }
   // Decrease time by one second
   if (--psecond < 0) {
     psecond = 59;
     if (--pminute < 0) {
       pminute = 59;
       if (--phour < 0) {
         phour = 23;
         if (--pday < 0) {
           pday = 0;
         }
       }
     }
   }
   var minute = ((pminute < 10) ? "0" : "") + pminute;
   var second = ((psecond < 10) ? "0" : "") + psecond;
   var day = "";
   var hour = "";
   if (phour > 0) {
   hour = ((phour < 10) ? "0" : "") + phour + ":";
   }
   if (pday > 0) {
     day = pday + ":";
   }
   if (pday <= 0) {
     if (phour <= 0) {
       hour = "";
     }
   }
   document.getElementById(id).innerHTML = day + hour + minute + ":" + second;
   time = time - 1;
   // Recurse timer
   var command = "countDown('" + id + "'," + time + ")";
   ForwardTimerID[id] = setTimeout(command, 1000);
 }
               </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        var currenttime = "June 21, 2018 20:06:00"
                var serverdate= new Date(currenttime)
 
                function padlength(zero) {
                  var output=(zero.toString().length==1)? "0"+zero : zero
                  return output
                }
                function displaytime() {
                  serverdate.setSeconds(serverdate.getSeconds()+1)
                  var timestring = padlength(serverdate.getHours()) + ":" + padlength(serverdate.getMinutes())
                  document.getElementById("footerservertime").innerHTML=timestring
                  if (document.getElementById("servertime")) {
                    document.getElementById("servertime").innerHTML=timestring
                  }
                }
                setInterval("displaytime()", 1000);
       </script>
       <div class="time-block">
        <span id="footerservertime">
        </span>
       </div>

    <script>
     function isIE () {
         var myNav = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
         return (myNav.indexOf("msie") != -1) ? parseInt(myNav.split("msie")[1]) : false;
       }
       function isChrome () {
         var myNavChrome = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
         return (myNavChrome.indexOf("chrome") != -1) ? parseInt(myNavChrome.split("chrome/")[1]) : false;
       }
       function isFirefox () {
         var myNavFirefox = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
         return (myNavFirefox.indexOf("firefox") != -1) ? parseInt(myNavFirefox.split("firefox/")[1]) : false;
       }
       if (isIE () && isIE () < 10) {
          window.location.href = "/sorry-please-upgrade" //redirect
       }
       if (isChrome () && isChrome () < 24) {
          window.location.href = "/sorry-please-upgrade" //redirect
       }
       if (isFirefox () && isFirefox () < 28) {
          window.location.href = "/sorry-please-upgrade" //redirect
       }
    </script>
